<div id="review_3125397576" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3125397576" />
    <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers"><img alt="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581473939p2/74622641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3125397576?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers">Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=contem-new-adult-romance">contem-new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=h-s-that-cheated-or-cheats">h-s-that-cheated-or-cheats</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=erotic-bdsm">erotic-bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=dom-sub">dom-sub</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3125397576" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer309844477412568999">Not entirely sure what to say about this book. But I'll begin by noting:<br/><br/><b>THIS IS NOT A ROMANCE.<br/><br/>It's psychological drama. The sex in this book is not at all "hot." It's about power and dominance and submission and making a point and all the other stuff but never about LOVE.</b><br/><br/>Given that this is not a romance (which makes it a book I don't typically read), and it's not about love, (which makes the writing have to work that much harder for me to like it), it wasn't bad.<br/><br/>There were moments when it was ri</span>
  <span id="freeText309844477412568999" style="display:none">Not entirely sure what to say about this book. But I'll begin by noting:<br /><br /><b>THIS IS NOT A ROMANCE.<br /><br />It's psychological drama. The sex in this book is not at all "hot." It's about power and dominance and submission and making a point and all the other stuff but never about LOVE.</b><br /><br />Given that this is not a romance (which makes it a book I don't typically read), and it's not about love, (which makes the writing have to work that much harder for me to like it), it wasn't bad.<br /><br />There were moments when it was riveting. For about 40% of it. But then it got kinda boring. And there was a whole 2 weeks in between me starting the book and finishing it. I was never tempted to come back to it all the while, which says something.<br /><br />Nora/ Eleanor is in love with Soren, a Catholic priest. They have a Dom-sub thing going, and he beats her and has rough sex with her but loves her more than anyone else.<br /><br />She's been broken up with him for years. But they can't help but circle each other like they always do. And he still takes "liberties" with her whenever they're together. <b>It's like he's an owner who lets his little bitch dog sniff at other people, but she'd always be his bitch.</b><br /><br />(Wow, reading Book 2, and boy did I peg their relationship! Glad I didn't miss the point...)<br /><br />Nora writes erotica and wants to get published by a big firm, so she gets herself the best editor. Zach. Who is separated from his wife but still married. His wife Grace has apparently moved on before he's fully left her with a guy named Ian. But Zach has been celibate for over a year.<br /><br />Until, of course, the seductive, playful, dangerous Nora. They do end up having sex, BTW. And it even becomes a means through which Zach gets back with his wife, who never stopped loving him and he never stopped loving her.<br /><br />The worst of all this drama happened to the innocent virgin, hung-like-a-horse young god named Wesley, who is Nora's best friend and assistant and lives with her. He's in love with her too. He's like the angel to Soren's devil. They are both blond and hung. <br /><br />She ends up making him leave, because she realizes that he'd have to become someone he's not to be with her. Deep down, she's "twisted" - she loves being owned and beaten. She loves Soren. And while Wesley makes her feel like herself, Soren makes her feel like his.<br /><br />And in the end, Nora doesn't want to be "herself" she wants to be dominated and "his."<br /><br />This was a pretty long book to go through all that gymnastics above. Pretty sure I'm not going to read more in this series.<br /><br />Writing was intelligent and good, but I find the story simply didn't resonate with me. I guess this simply isn't my genre.</span>
  <a data-text-id="309844477412568999" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16030705486320128141"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg' width='200' height='150' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After finishing 13 hours of audiobook, I feel a strange sense of loss now that I'm done with this book. "The Siren" crushed and destroyed all of my expectations. It was nothing like I had anticipated. <br/><br/>It is NOT:<br/><br/><b>Erotica<br/>A traditional romance novel<br/>Cliche-ridden</b><br/><br/>Let me break it down for you. This book is Tiffany Reisz writing a novel about an author writing an erotic novel. Confused yet? I was. I was expecting a down and dirty explicit BDSM erotic romance. That is not at all what I got. Though the co</span>
  <span id="freeText16030705486320128141" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After finishing 13 hours of audiobook, I feel a strange sense of loss now that I'm done with this book. "The Siren" crushed and destroyed all of my expectations. It was nothing like I had anticipated. <br><br>It is NOT:<br><br><b>Erotica<br>A traditional romance novel<br>Cliche-ridden</b><br><br>Let me break it down for you. This book is Tiffany Reisz writing a novel about an author writing an erotic novel. Confused yet? I was. I was expecting a down and dirty explicit BDSM erotic romance. That is not at all what I got. Though the content is taboo (it can't get much more taboo, honestly, without the addition of incest), there is very little on page sex. What sex content is shown is surprisingly, shockingly tasteful. <br><br>Much of the actual book mirrors what Nora (the erotic author and main character) is going through in the writing of her novel. The sex scenes serve only to further the plot line (like Nora's editor told her to do)- nothing is gratuitous. In fact, this story is edited to perfection. It is really and truly flawless in its execution. <br><br>What I liked best about this book is that it is the overlapping plot lines that sort of seamlessly come together in the end. There is Zach, the editor having serious marital issues, Nora and her torrid relationship with Soren and Wes, Nora and her writing process, and the whole BDSM dynamic that colors each relationship (for good or for bad). The different story lines don't interfere with one another but rather help progress each other. <br><br>Nora is a complicated and compelling character that will stick with me for a long time. I found her to be utterly fascinating. However, that brings me to why my rating is 4 stars instead of 5 stars. I felt very detached from Nora. I was not emotionally invested in her or rest of the characters. Mentally, I was so intrigued and loved the story, but it was more from a clinical point of view. I never grew teary eyed or screamed or got nervous- it was all in my head and not in my heart, I'm afraid. I adored the story but it wasn't an emotional read for me. <br><br>A word about the audio version of this book: I loved, loved the narrator for this one. His Zach and Grace voices were flawless, as was his Soren voice. I even forgive him the iffy Nora voice and the HORRIBLE Wes accent because he did such a perfect job narrating the rest of the story. My favorite narrator on any audiobook thus far. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16030705486320128141" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_433215417" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/433215417" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/433215417?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer433215417" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16436591421436570706"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "If you come back to me," he said, "will you run or will you crawl?"<br/><br/>"I'll fly..."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394164ra/758868.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><br/><i>This is not a romance book...</i><br/><br/><b>It is, however, a story about love, friendship, faith and about discovering all your darkest, deepest desires and learning how to deal with them.</b> <br/><br/>When I started reading <i>The Siren</i>, I didn't really have any expectations about how the story would develop or where it all led up to. But after a while, I found myself being more and more enthralled by the storyline and its many</span>
  <span id="freeText16436591421436570706" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "If you come back to me," he said, "will you run or will you crawl?"<br><br>"I'll fly..."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394164ra/758868.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><i>This is not a romance book...</i><br><br><b>It is, however, a story about love, friendship, faith and about discovering all your darkest, deepest desires and learning how to deal with them.</b> <br><br>When I started reading <i>The Siren</i>, I didn't really have any expectations about how the story would develop or where it all led up to. But after a while, I found myself being more and more enthralled by the storyline and its many different, captivating characters. I ended up really enjoying this well written and darkly enticing story and I became a fan of the author Tiffany Reisz' lyrical writing style.<br><br><b>
  <u>The Story</u>
</b><br><br><b>Nora Sutherlin</b>, our main character, is one of America's most famous and most notorious writers of erotic novels. She's blunt, sarcastic and very witty and by far one of my favorite characters in the book. They call her <b>The Siren</b>, but why? That is for you to find out by reading the story...<br><br>When Nora decides it is time for her to pursue a different carrier path by writing her first more serious, main stream novel; she ends up being taken under the wings of one of the best editors in the country, Zachary Easton. He's the one who holds Nora's future as a writer in his very demanding hands; and he's not afraid to use the power he has over her.<br><br>As soon as Nora and Zach begin working together, they find that there's an attraction between them, they can't seem to ignore. The more they get to know each other, the more they find out about each others darkest secrets and desires. In the world of Nora Sutherlin, love and romance are two very different things. To her love equals pain.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"If you're a sadomaochist, pain feels like love to you. Not being hurt is what hurts."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>After spending 13 years of her life as a submissive to the extremely powerful Dom Søren, she is now a Dominatrix of her own and she decides to introduce Zach to her BDSM lifestyle. Together they try to move on from the past they left behind; Zach is still having a hard time letting go of the wife he's technically still married to, but who lives across the ocean in England and who he barely speaks to anymore. And Nora, who still feels a deep love towards her ex Søren, finds herself having a hard time staying away from the grip Søren still holds on her life...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"There are only two reasons why you leave someone you're still in love with - either it's the right thing to do, or it's the only thing to do."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And then there's Wesley, Nora's nineteen-year-old assistant and roommate at the same time. His character turned out to be, to me at least, the one that managed to brighten up the story with his innocence, his sense of humor and his ability to be strong and caring even at such a young age. He doesn't approve of Nora's sadomasochistic lifestyle and all he wants is for her to be happy and to never get hurt again.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Every day you battle an enemy I cannot fight with you or for you. But if there is ever a chance for repreive, then I will bear you across the world on my back to see you finally at peace."<br><br>"But what if the enemy you think I fight isn't the enemy at all? What if this enemy is only me?"<br><br>"Then I will save you from yourself."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Thoughts</u>
</b><br><br>The Siren is mostly about Nora and her relationship with the different men in her life. It's a very complex and fascinating story and unlike any other book I've ever read. Some parts of it are dark and may seem really brutal to read but overall the author wrote it in a very compelling, sensual way that did not leave me reeling with disgust or anger towards any of the characters. You should however know that the story doesn't end with a HEA, at least not this first part of the story. Therefore, I will definitely read the rest of the Original Sinners series as well to find out what happens next in the life of Nora, aka The Siren, and all "her" men...<br><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quote</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"The same wind that blows us off course can turn and carry us home."<br><br>~</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394164ra/758869.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><br><br>****<br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16436591421436570706" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15835198-the-siren">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=continuing-plot">continuing-plot</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449242687" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7959770516430626544"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764754.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Writing erotica is like fucking someone for the first time. You aren't sure exactly what he wants yet so you try to give him everything he could possibly want. Everything and anything...You hit every nerve and eventually you'll hit the nerve. Have I hit any nerves yet?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764755.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is NOT a romance novel. It is NOT sunshine and rainbows, pretty and light, sweet and romantic. <br/><br/>It's dark, painful, erotic, beautifully sadistic, captivating, and unlike anything I've read before.<br/><br/>I'll start by say</span>
  <span id="freeText7959770516430626544" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764754.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Writing erotica is like fucking someone for the first time. You aren't sure exactly what he wants yet so you try to give him everything he could possibly want. Everything and anything...You hit every nerve and eventually you'll hit the nerve. Have I hit any nerves yet?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764755.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is NOT a romance novel. It is NOT sunshine and rainbows, pretty and light, sweet and romantic. <br><br>It's dark, painful, erotic, beautifully sadistic, captivating, and unlike anything I've read before.<br><br>I'll start by saying that had I not immediately read, The Angel, right after this, I might not have felt the same about it. I think reading the next book helped put a lot of things that were tough to swallow in perspective for me. This is definitely not your mama's romance novel. There are parts I read that were incredibly tough to swallow, but I loved every darkly erotic page of it.<br><br>Nora Sutherlin is a famous erotica writer, but she is determined for her new book to be different, more personal, but she needs help.<br><br>Zachary Easton is known as "The London Fog" in the editing world for a reason. He's demanding, brutally honest, and not really known for his bright and chipper personality. When he agrees to take on Nora's manuscript, even though he views her as the guttersnipe author, he does so on one condition. Nora must rewrite her entire novel to his standards in six weeks.<br><br>Forced to enter her world, Zach soon finds there is so much more to Nora that what he initially thought.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764756.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nora is not just an erotica writer. She's a dominatrix, and a famous one at that.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764757.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But behind the veil of leather, high heels, and whips, Nora is also so much more. While I loved her quirky personality, and snarky humor, we also gets snippets of her 'other' side when she is around Wesley.<br><br>Wesley was my favorite part about this book. I just adored him. He's Nora's intern/roomate, and just so happens that he's a 19 year old virgin. We get a glimpse inside Nora's softer side when she is around him. Wesley hates the dominatrix part of Nora's life. He doesn't understand the appeal of that dark world, particularly when given Nora's history with Soren.<br><br>Soren...WOW! I don't even know where to begin with Soren. <br><blockquote>
  <b>He could read a soul with the merest glance. He'd know what she would become from the moment he first saw her. He had told her so. It had always been her favorite bedtime story.</b>
</blockquote><br>Soren and Nora were lovers for 13 years<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Soren and I aren't a romance. We're just a fantasy." </b>
</blockquote><br>That is until Nora left him, over a year ago. Though they still have a somewhat relationship... <br><blockquote>
  <b>Soren isn't some boyfriend you have a fight with and then kiss and make up. He's the invading army you surrender to before it burns your village down.</b>
</blockquote><br>I hated him. I was intrigued with him. I hated the fact that I was intrigued with him. At first what we get are Nora's flashbacks, and they were no easier to deal with than the reality of finally meeting Soren.<br>When the reality of all that he is finally came to light, I was left utterly speechless.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764758._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Then there is also the mysterious Kingsley. Kingsley, Nora, and Soren have a very convuluted past that we don't get much of an explanation for in this book, but mere glimpes. One thing was clear, however...<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Nora's not just some smut writer with a wild sex life. She's the motherfucking queen of the Underground. And Kingsley Edge is, obviously, our king."<br>"And him? What is he?" Zach didn't even want to say Soren's name.<br>"He's whatever's higher than a king and queen."<br>"An emperor?" Zach guessed.<br>"A god."</b>
</blockquote><br>The writing is absolutely, fucking brilliant! The story mainly focuses on Zach and Nora, but Wesley, Soren, ad Kingsley do take a somewhat role in the book as well. We do't get much of a backstory in this book on anyone other than Zach.<br><br>I really loved Zach's character. He was obviously still struggling over his marriage falling apart, and still being in love with his wife. But in his work with Nora, he begins to develop feelings for her that he has a very hard time dealing with.<br><blockquote>
  <b>Nora...the siren and the goddess, the ship and the wine-dark sea. She would either save him or end him. Right now, with her words singing in his ears, he didn't really care which.</b>
</blockquote><br>Nora, I believe, was a big reason as to why I was hesitant in reading this book at first. I don't usually enjoy stories with Domme's. It's just not my thing. But Nora was so much more than I anticipated. She's somewhat an enigma in this book. We get to see her dark edge, and her soft side as well. She's obviously struggling with knowing that she will never be comfortable in a Vanilla relationship, yet yearning to be with Wesley at the same time while knowing she can't. She's still drawn to Soren, and their connection.<br><br>I loved the way the author weaved all of these character's stories together. It was beautifully and flawlessly done. <br><br>I don't want to reveal too much, you simply must read this to figure things out for yourself. But I will say that is one of the most captivating books I have read in a long, long time. <br><br><b>4.5 Brilliantly Sadistic Stars</b><br><br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7959770516430626544" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2178602648" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2178602648" />
    <a title="Evgeny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9340136-evgeny"><img alt="Evgeny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544797852p2/9340136.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2178602648?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Evgeny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Evgeny" href="/user/show/9340136-evgeny">Evgeny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15835198-the-siren">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9340136-evgeny?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9340136-evgeny?shelf=adventure">adventure</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2178602648" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2867896759228600169">Zachary Easton was a Brit living in NYC where he ran off to in order to escape his personal demons. He was working as an editor (a very good editor) in a publishing house (a well-known one). One day his boss J.P. trying to revive weak book sales decided to publish an erotica book. He picked a famous - among erotica readers - writer working in the genre Nora Sutherlin and Zach as her editor. Poor Zack initially thought editing such a book is beneath him, but J.P. told him to do it or else. As we </span>
  <span id="freeText2867896759228600169" style="display:none">Zachary Easton was a Brit living in NYC where he ran off to in order to escape his personal demons. He was working as an editor (a very good editor) in a publishing house (a well-known one). One day his boss J.P. trying to revive weak book sales decided to publish an erotica book. He picked a famous - among erotica readers - writer working in the genre Nora Sutherlin and Zach as her editor. Poor Zack initially thought editing such a book is beneath him, but J.P. told him to do it or else. As we all know when you boss tells you to do something you do it. Or else. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574819976i/28516173.jpg" alt="Boss" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Other than being an erotica writer, Nora also had a reputation of being completely outrageous in real life. For example the rumor was, she was living with an underage boy. No wonder Zach was afraid to meet her even though he did his best to hide it when the said meeting finally happened. Zach had no clue how deep the rabbit hole went - the one he was about to fall into. And neither had I. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574819913i/28516166.png" alt="Rabbit hole" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My first impression about the book was the writing quality. it was better than about 90% of contemporary romance/erotica books. My second impression would be a warning for people that think about reading it: <i>the book will drag kicking and screaming you way out of your comfort zone</i>. You have been warned and I am dead serious here. By the time you finish reading your comfort zone will be invisible over the horizon. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574820137i/28516200.jpg" alt="Comfort Zone" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Characters: Zach was great and fleshed out, Nora was even better and fleshed out, Wes was good and somewhat fleshed out, and Søren was... Søren (spoiler, spoiler). Even some of the minor characters were at least not boring. The story was interesting and kept me curious through the whole length. The sex scenes were not too many, but those were... I am not going to spoil it. Comfort zone - remember? As far as I am concerned there was only one problem with the story (and none with characters).<br><br>This has became practically a staple of any romance book; I challenge anybody to find any without the following. One person holds a deep dark secret from his/her partner thinking, "I will reveal it as soon as stuff happens". Before the stuff happens the partner learns about the secret in the worst possible way and the lack of timely communication blows in both of their faces. I saw this coming from literally the first chapter and was not surprised by the fallout in the least. Oh well, you cannot ask for a perfection.<br><br>Other than occasional (but not ordinary) sexual interludes Zach and Nora were working together as a writer and an editor. This book finally gave me some idea about what editors are supposed to do. This in turn made me understand why 99.9% of self-published books are pure undiluted crap. Also it left me wondering what some of the editors of some of traditionally published books charged money for. Wrong genre, but I would love to have a chat with a person who edited a well-known popular modern fantasy series asking him three questions: how much did you get paid? what exactly did you do with these books? WHY DID YOU NOT DO YOUR JOB???<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574820211i/28516202._SX540_.jpg" alt="Sleeping" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you are still brave enough to try reading the book after all I just said, come up with a safe word, always keep it in mind and be ready to stop reading if things get too much for you. There will not be a comfort zone to retreat back to. The rating is <b>4.5 stars</b>, but I feel it is closer to full 5 than 4, so weak 5 stars it is: not perfect, but very good. <br><br>P.S. Looking at the number of books in the series I suspect Tiffany Reisz turned it into a cash cow (or a retirement plan). <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574820373i/28516207._SX540_.png" alt="Cash Cow" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>In any way, the first book is self-contained and I can pretend it is standalone. I am not sure if I will ever read the second installment. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2867896759228600169" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1084804482" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1084804482" />
    <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review"><img alt="Peek At My Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1414761368p2/18263404.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1084804482?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Peek At My Book Review" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review">Peek At My Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review?shelf=2012">2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1084804482" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13075607140531645963"><b>Rating : 3.5 ‘Don’t judge a book by its mother. Just read.’ Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420721724i/13255502._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='310' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>My Views :</b> First wring a book about an author is something that I haven’t read before, to see all the trouble that they have to take phew <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398993280ra/9495104.gif' width='40' height='50' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> ….The first half of the book wasn’t much and to be honest I was getting pretty bored but the next half was quite entertaining. I was Not captivated or enthralled by this one and I must say that I’m quite disappointed as I’ve heard great things about this series. <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420804323i/13267666.png' width='40' height='40' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Both Zach and Nora lived differe</span>
  <span id="freeText13075607140531645963" style="display:none"><b>Rating : 3.5 ‘Don’t judge a book by its mother. Just read.’ Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420721724i/13255502._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My Views :</b> First wring a book about an author is something that I haven’t read before, to see all the trouble that they have to take phew <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398993280ra/9495104.gif" width="40" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> ….The first half of the book wasn’t much and to be honest I was getting pretty bored but the next half was quite entertaining. I was Not captivated or enthralled by this one and I must say that I’m quite disappointed as I’ve heard great things about this series. <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420804323i/13267666.png" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Both Zach and Nora lived different lives from the beginning. One could see that their previous lives had an impact on their present and in a way it was still ruling their lives…Then we have got Westley who was the sweet boy, he is the one who brings some control in Nora’s life. After that we’ve got Soren, I was appalled when I learnt the identity of Soren but he wowed me. I wanted more of him in the book. There was no real romance going on in the book just Sex. Overall the book was Okay…<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491989350ra/22469640.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Style of writing :</b> This is the third book that I’ve read by this author and I love her style of writing. She is witty and funny. It was easy to read, what I loved most was the wit she used with Nora…When Nora writes her story with Soren, it feels like how versatile a writer Tiffany Reisz is and I loved it. I loved the twists in the story they managed to make me keep read the book.<br><br><b>Characters :</b> I loved Nora from the beginning as she was someone clever and I loved how she made Zach Blush. But later on she turned out to be the character that I hated most throughout the book. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420804252ra/13267644.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Nora was a fantastic writer and an even better Dom (even though we do not get much of her Dom side). But her decisions concerning Westley made mem hate her. She was so engrossed in saving herself that she managed to hurt/harm Westley.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Better to reign in hell than serve in Heaven.” </i>
</b><br><br> Zach for me was not the real protagonist of the story, he was just there to help Nora with the book and sort out certain things in her life. Then Nora helped to settle his but nothing more. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Your orders,” she said. “You told me to stop writing what I knew and start writing what I wanted to know. I want to know…you.” She took a step closer and Zach’s heart dropped a few feet and landed somewhere in the vicinity of his groin. </i>
</b><br><br>As for Westley <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/475086.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> I wished we had more background information about him; I felt like I didn’t get to understand the relationship between Wes and Nora. Westley was such a sweet boy, sometimes stupid but I really felt for him at the end of the book…thanks to Bitch Nora. <br><br>As for Soren, I absolutely Adore him. For me this book was more about Nora and the aftermath of her relationship with Soren.<br><br><b>Favorite Part :</b> <b>
  <i>“It was my mistake—” he turned and met her eyes “—thinking we had all the time in the world.”..</i>
</b> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491989350i/22469641.png" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> (This was said by Soren...He was actually the reason I kept on reading the book till the end.)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420804402i/13267672._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did not work?</b> There were certain things that were disturbing:<br>1.	The F/F scenes that was present. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396994ra/765645.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> That was my first and I was a little uncomfortable but since they were very brief it was okay…But I Was Not Warned!!!<br><br>2.	The fact that Nora being the heroine of the book sleeps with so many men and women in the book was awkward. I couldn’t understand her feelings properly toward each character that she sleeps with (except for the subs) and why she wanted to sleep with them!!! <span>[image error]</span> <br><br>3.	Who Nora truly Loved??? I felt like it was all the three men in her life.<br><br><b> Similar books? </b> None..<br><br><b> Recommended :</b> Hmm…yes, the book wasn’t bad just a bit complicated to understand. It was quite boring in the beginning for me but changed around 50% but I started really enjoying it only after 80%...To say the climax!!!<br><br><a href="http://peekatmybookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="87" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418569189i/12827092._SX540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img alt="description" height="60" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418815952i/12909809.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_362835035" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/362835035" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/362835035?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781459234499" href="/book/show/14623986-the-siren">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Open minded readers</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Karla by: </span>
      Michelle, Searock, Taryn and countless other GR friends! 
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=sensual">sensual</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=angst-filled">angst-filled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=disturbing">disturbing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=larger-than-life-character">larger-than-life-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=pain">pain</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=heartbreaking">heartbreaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=hurtful">hurtful</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=spunky-heroine">spunky-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=tortured-souls">tortured-souls</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=series-introduction">series-introduction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer362835035" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16838159051072607209">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><b>5 Head Spinning Stars!!</b> Although some of the subject matter in this book was not always comfortable to read about, I was <b>ENTHRALLED</b> and had to keep reading. A book that does that is worth 5 STARS from me and then some!!<br/><br/><b>si•ren: a seductively beautiful or charming woman, especially one who beguiles men, aka Nora Sutherlin.</b><br/><br/>I honestly don’t even know where to begin with this book, nor how to write a review that gives <i>The Siren</i> and Tiffany Reisz the proper adula</span>
  <span id="freeText16838159051072607209" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><b>5 Head Spinning Stars!!</b> Although some of the subject matter in this book was not always comfortable to read about, I was <b>ENTHRALLED</b> and had to keep reading. A book that does that is worth 5 STARS from me and then some!!<br /><br /><b>si•ren: a seductively beautiful or charming woman, especially one who beguiles men, aka Nora Sutherlin.</b><br /><br />I honestly don’t even know where to begin with this book, nor how to write a review that gives <i>The Siren</i> and Tiffany Reisz the proper adulations. There are circumstances in this book that arise that I would normally condone, but the author makes us comprehend and accept that not all situations warrant the same handling. The unconventional, the taboo, is justified in a way that the pain of the characters is your pain and in their shoes you would probably resort to the same extreme measures and means to alleviate and re-gain control over your life. Or, to help someone find their way back…relieve them of their anguish…give them something to live for. I'm making sense and no sense at all and that is exactly how this book made me feel. Turned my thinking topsy-turvy, what was so wrong in my mind became so right. The writing is nothing short of <b>BRILLIANT!!!</b><br /><br />It delves into the darkest realm of BDSM, but isn’t overrun with play by play action like most books in this genre. Oh, that’s not to say that the book doesn’t have its erotic scenes in the BDSM setting or otherwise, but it’s not the focus of the story. You get a taste of what these characters are about, yet it's not excessively graphic. It’s the main element in the story; however it takes a back seat. This book deals with inner turmoil, self-discovery, acceptance and sacrifice. <br /><br />Front and center is one Nora Sutherlin, one of the most compelling characters I’ve ever had the pleasure to read about. An erotic book author, she is charming, thoughtful, caring, determined, inquisitive, funny and hides a secret only known to those who are a part of “her world”. Zachary Easton, much to his dismay, has been assigned to edit Nora’s book. In his eyes Nora’s books have no worth and are a waste of his time. All that changes as he comes to understand Nora and the alternate world that she rules. As the layers of Zach’s snooty façade are peeled back we find a man in pain and in need of what only Nora is capable of giving him. Wesley, oh Wesley… so much more mature than your nineteen years. It’s a fine line that he teeters on with Nora, theirs is a true love, but are they meant to be lovers? Their relationship was compelling to say the least. The one character that I wanted to abhor, hate, despise, ended up being the one that seized my attention and gained my respect…<b>Soren!!</b> How could someone with such authority and position do what he does and come off like a saint?! His initial appearance in the book had me gaping, eyes wide, breathless, I wanted to throw myself at his feet, do as he commanded, and then <b>follow him to hell and back!!</b> Tiffany Riesz what have you done to me??? <br /><br />If you don’t like to think outside the box or have an open mind, then this is not the book for you. <b>BUT</b> if you can be objective, deal with the unexpected, then strap yourself in, throw caution to the wind, throw your arms in the air and <i>The Siren</i> will take you on an emotional rollercoaster ride that is guaranteed to make your head spin and turn your world upside down!! <br /><br />I’ve posted partial lyrics to the song <i>Pain</i> by Three Days Grace. In my opinion it expresses what some of the characters in <i>The Siren</i> are feeling, it kept playing in my head as I was reading and could be the book's anthem.<br /><br /><i>You're sick of feeling numb<br />You're not the only one<br />I'll take you by the hand<br />And I'll show you a world that you can understand<br />This life is filled with hurt<br />When happiness doesn't work<br />Trust me and take my hand<br /><br />Pain, without love<br />Pain, I can't get enough<br />Pain, I like it rough<br />'Cause I'd rather feel pain than nothing at all<br /><br />Anger and agony<br />Are better than misery<br />Trust me I've got a plan<br />When the lights go off you will understand<br /><br />I know <br />That you're wounded<br />You know <br />That I'm here to save you<br />You know <br />I'm always here for you<br />I know <br />That you'll thank me later<br /><br />Pain, without love<br />Pain, I can't get enough<br />Pain, I like it rough<br />'Cause I'd rather feel pain than nothing at all<br /></i><br />Adam Gontier/Three Days Grace<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Ud4HuAzHEUc">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Ud4HuA...</a><br /><br /><br /><i> ARC courtesy of Harlequin Publishing via NetGalley</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16838159051072607209" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer921114682" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17805871501636504315"><b>6 welcome to the 8th circle STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418898744i/12939862.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A love story is not the same as a romance novel. A romance novel is the story of two people falling in love against their will. This is a story of two people who leave each other against their will. It starts to end the minute they meet.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><i>**Buddy-Re-Read December 2014 with my girls Jasmine, Eda and Supreet. I updated my review with pretty pictures, tweaked it a little here and there (added a book summary and a few comments etc.), but I don't really ha</i></span>
  <span id="freeText17805871501636504315" style="display:none"><b>6 welcome to the 8th circle STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418898744i/12939862.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A love story is not the same as a romance novel. A romance novel is the story of two people falling in love against their will. This is a story of two people who leave each other against their will. It starts to end the minute they meet.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>**Buddy-Re-Read December 2014 with my girls Jasmine, Eda and Supreet. I updated my review with pretty pictures, tweaked it a little here and there (added a book summary and a few comments etc.), but I don't really have anything else to add to my original thoughts about the characters. I'm still madly in love with this book, maybe even more so now that I know what happens next. I just find myself smiling all of the time while I'm reading. I definitely recommend a re-read for those of you who haven't done that yet.</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy Shit! I’ve never read anything like this and I’m so glad I finally succumbed to temptation and picked up <i>The Siren</i>.<br><br>I was very reluctant at first because I didn’t think Nora being a Domme would be something I could enjoy reading. But colour me surprised...Nora actually makes my favourite-book-heroines list. <br><br>I read <i>The Gift</i> before <i>The Siren</i> and I have to blame a slight brain freeze, but I didn’t make the connection that Elli (Eleanor) and Nora is the same girl. Even the first time Søren called her Eleanor I didn’t get it. I read on and then it hit me, I went back and after that I had to take a short coffee break and try to put those two characters together. I love her even more now. <br><br><i>**Totally useless information, but since I had it in my original review I just kept it.</i><br>But anyway...let's see what this is all about:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Erotica author Nora Sutherlin has a few problems and they all involve men.<br><br>There is her new British editor Zachary Easton, who thinks of her more as a guttersnipe and less as an author. But despite his reservations he agrees to work with her, but under some demanding time restrictions and a lot of pressure.<br><br>Then we have the nine-teen year old student/friend/potential boy-toy Wesley who has been living with her for a year now.<br><br>And then there is the man she left five years ago. Søren.<br><br>That's all you need to know for now, for more information...READ THE DAMN BOOK!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418910941i/12944190.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You merely think you know her. It’s one of her best tricks. She flirts, she teases, she confesses everything but reveals nothing. It’s the oldest magician’s trick—smoke and mirrors, misdirection… You are absolutely certain she’s here, when all the while she’s right over here…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Nora is such a fun and yet complicated character. I loved being in her head, because she is so independent, bold and unapologetic. I don’t think I’ve seen a character like her in an Erotica book before and what a refreshing turn of events that is, really. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418900517i/12940073.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It's not morning until you're awake. And it's not night until you're asleep in your bed under my roof. And I could go on and on but hope is a horrible thing, and I love you too much to give you any.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Wes. Oh Wes. He is so sweet and such a good boy, and as it happens it’s also the problem I have with him. My twisted mind doesn’t compute with the good, sweet and loving guys. Give me a Søren any time of the day and I’m in.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418903142i/12941584.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“To Zachary Easton, my editor. Fuck you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Zach. I love this character and I love his ‘relationship/friendship’ with Nora. He is the perfect conduit to get a glimpse into this world Nora lives in and I’m a huge fan of how this whole thing worked out for them. Just one minor thing, or a question really...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Please, someone tell me there is going to be some more Zach in the following books. I want more! ....<i>**now that I'm re-reading this I just want to hug myself and tell me that everything will be alright and that I will be laughing so hard by the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17251444-the-mistress" rel="nofollow noopener">The Mistress</a>...oh good times. ;D </i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418900517i/12940074.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Søren isn’t some boyfriend you have a fight with and then kiss and make up. He’s the invading army you surrender to before it burns your village down.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Søren. Oh man, that one is intense. I seriously have to read on before I can say anything about him. But he sure is one of the most intriguing and infuriating book characters I’ve ever come across. I can already tell I will be irrevocably in love with him by the time this series is done. <br><br><i>**and I was right. I am so in love with this man, but I didn't need to finish the series before I came to the conclusion. There really is no one like him...oh Søren. *sigh*</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If you come back to me," he said, making a rare concession, "will you run or crawl?"<br><br>Nora had pressed her whole body into him at that moment. Resting her head on his strong shoulder, she watched as a tear forged a river down his long and muscled back. <br><br>"I'll fly.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Oh you better, girlfriend! Or I know a bunch of ladies who will. ;D<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And last but not least a word to the author. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4480131.Tiffany_Reisz" title="Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">Tiffany Reisz</a> is like the Erotica/BDSM whisperer. There is no one like her and she really takes this overdone genre and spins it on its head and she does it with excellent writing on top of that, which happens to be a hit miss in this genre as well. I’m in awe and I swear I will read anything this woman publishes. If she happens to write a cook book...I will buy it. No questions asked.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1871699867" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer515232041151330255"><br/><b>RATING: 4 "Welcome to the Eighth Circle" Hearts!!</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The same wind that blows us off course can turn and carry us home.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><i>The Siren</i> is a work of contradictions; both light and dark, seductive and conservative, passionate and humble, tender and chaotic. There is not much I can say about this beyond what has already been said; the writing is flawless, evocative and beautiful in its prose. It hooks you with every word read and every page turned, bringing out turbulent emotions both good and </span>
  <span id="freeText515232041151330255" style="display:none"><br /><b>RATING: 4 "Welcome to the Eighth Circle" Hearts!!</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The same wind that blows us off course can turn and carry us home.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><i>The Siren</i> is a work of contradictions; both light and dark, seductive and conservative, passionate and humble, tender and chaotic. There is not much I can say about this beyond what has already been said; the writing is flawless, evocative and beautiful in its prose. It hooks you with every word read and every page turned, bringing out turbulent emotions both good and bad. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If you come back to me," he said, making a rare concession, "will you run or crawl?"<br /><br />Nora had pressed her whole body into him at that moment. Resting her head on his strong shoulder, she watched as a tear forged a river down his long and muscled back. <br /><br />"I'll fly.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />The characters are complex and unravel as the story continues (though not entirely, and I've been ensured that they will with each subsequent book). Nora, at first, I loved her spunk and power as a woman, her grace as a woman, but towards the end, she made me angry. I didn't understand some of her actions. Wes, this sweet boy is one of my favourite parts of this story. Kingsley is mysterious, and I want to know more about him. Had it not been for Nora and Zach being so utterly devoted to their significant others, I would've loved them as a couple. And at last... Søren...I don't know him enough to say whether I like him or not yet, but from his actions so far, I don't understand him, his lifestyle or his needs. I'm hoping that clarifies with upcoming books.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It's not morning until you're awake. And it's not night until you're asleep in your bed under my roof. And I could go on and on but hope is a horrible thing, and I love you too much to give you any.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><br />Looking forward to <i>The Angel</i> next! <br /><br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>Posted: January 15, 2017</b>

<div id="review_337087878" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/337087878" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/337087878?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/3361149-kay">Kay</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=romantica-or-erotica">romantica-or-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=dark-or-taboo">dark-or-taboo</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer337087878" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9740712888238148420"><i>Adult review for very dark/somewhat taboo erotic content.</i> <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Verbal abuse? Zach, where I come from 'slut' is a term of endearment. Want to see where I come from?"<br/><br/>"No."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>And so begins our tale of an erotica writer and her editor...or does it? You might want to throw out your preconceived notions of what to expect with this book because it's doubtful that any of your expectations will be met.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>The Players in our twisted game :<b></b></b>
</i><br/><br/><b>Nora</b> - She has three men by the balls, yet somehow can't seem </span>
  <span id="freeText9740712888238148420" style="display:none"><i>Adult review for very dark/somewhat taboo erotic content.</i> <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Verbal abuse? Zach, where I come from 'slut' is a term of endearment. Want to see where I come from?"<br /><br />"No."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />And so begins our tale of an erotica writer and her editor...or does it? You might want to throw out your preconceived notions of what to expect with this book because it's doubtful that any of your expectations will be met.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>The Players in our twisted game :<b></b></b>
</i><br /><br /><b>Nora</b> - She has three men by the balls, yet somehow can't seem to keep a firm grip on any of them.<br /><br /><b>Zach</b> - The editor with demons to exorcise.<br /><br /><b>Wesley</b> - The inexperienced virgin who just might know more than we give him credit for.<br /><br /><b>Soren</b> - Big bad. You hate him, you're intrigued by him, you know he's not one to be messed with.<br /><br /><b>Grace</b> - The ghost of a person who isn't even dead.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Ladies and Gentlemen! Step right up and watch as 'The Siren' singlehandedly wrecks havoc in the lives of our cast members. No admission fee required (except for the cost of the book)!</i>
</b><br /><br />If there's one thing that worked for this story, it was the curiosity factor. At first, I wasn't sure where we were headed. From the way the book starts, you automatically assume one thing. By the time you make it about halfway, you realize there's no way you can assume anything. There were definitely surprises a'plenty.<br /><br />I honestly couldn't find fault with the writing or the story. I'd been expecting a dark erotica but found that this read more like "mainstream literature reinterpreting erotica," which is interesting, considering that this was exactly what the female author character in the book was trying to do. We were wrapped in a story within a story and it made me wonder how much of <i>The Siren</i> came from Tiffany Reisz's own experience. That, to me, is a sign of accomplishment in writing.<br /><br />If you're wondering why I didn't go for a higher rating, I'll have to say that my own personal opinion of where the book should have gone did dampen my enthusiasm. With some books, the ending could be one I despised, yet I'm still able to award 5 stars because of an emotion brought out in me (yes, I have been pissed off at a book to the point of hatred and still felt it worthy of 5 stars). Unfortunately, the only emotion I felt when I came to the end was melancholy and not in "bawling my eyes out" sort of way. In this instance, melancholy just felt like a bit of a letdown. I saw the reason for the decision but failed to care for the solution.<br /><br />If the mixing of religious undertones and sexual overtures will make you uncomfortable, you'll want to stay away from this book. I can't say anything without giving a spoiler but expect some of that, along with some dark BDSM notes. <br /><br />For better or worse, this was an exquisitely written book. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"If you come back to me," he said, making a rare concession, "will you run or will you crawl?"<br /><br />Resting her head on his strong shoulder, she watched as a tear forged a river down his long and muscled back.<br /><br />"I'll fly."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="9740712888238148420" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <u> My Nora </u>

  <span id="freeText9202083243395388200" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <u> My Nora </u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797105i/627320._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u> My Soren </u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398286i/769582.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u> My Wes </u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797105i/627322._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“Romance is sex plus love. Erotica is sex plus fear."... and terrified I was! It is not a pretty story. It's a very complicated almost real life story. There are no obstacles of boulder size, there are Mount Everest size obstacles that ALL characters in this book face.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407015355i/10627895.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the story within the story that somewhat loosely paralleled the lives of the main characters. Nora lives and solves her life conundrums through writing. It is her therapy and she is her own psychologist. Amazingly strong she pulls herself out of her own hell and depression through her writing. She writes writes and deletes her love story with Soren to reminisce and remember. Gotta say it was not pretty and truly cringe worthy. But then again her 13 year old relationship with Soren is unconventional. But it is in their world and you just got to wrap your head around it and you do slowly and surely.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407015355i/10627896._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My favorite character was poor naive Wes. My heart broke for him as all his patience and optimism couldn't change nor bring Nora in his world. He is an amazing boy who will grow into a perfect man... but not a perfect man for Nora. Wes has a big part of her heart and her innocence that she will never reach and therefore they do not belong together (I hope I won't have to eat my words when this series concludes, but this is just my opinion).<br><br>Zach another important figure in her life most likely her creativity and one who helps her grow into a writer. She was a writer before but now she settles fully into her role with such confidence that I love it! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ even when he was an ass to her when he found out about her 2nd job. That anger &amp; despair he made her feel pushed her to finish that book. She didn't need his editing after all... well maybe some.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And I am so glad that his suffering only lasted just <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ this book aka 8months  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and I'm glad how things ended for him. I had Soren's precognition that although he has HOT chemistry with Nora he doesn't belong to her and she doesn't belong to him...<br><br>Now moving on to belonging... Soren... holy ssssss---- does he scared me in the begging. Shower scene anyone? But slowly he works into your system. He is still scary as hell but in a way you get him and his views and the world he lives in. But seriously!!! There are SOME VERY IMPORTANT things that's hard to wrap around. Won't spoil but those who read understand... *cough* profession wise.<br><br>To wrap up this rant... Loved the series very interested to know where this will lead.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398286ra/769585.gif" width="300" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><a href="http://wp.me/p4OeqO-wg" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer2204584370713555076">4.5--<b>Romance is sex plus love--Erotica is sex plus fear</b>--Stars!!!<br/><br/>First and foremost, I have absolutely no idea how to review this book.   <span id="freeText2204584370713555076" style="display:none">4.5--<b>Romance is sex plus love--Erotica is sex plus fear</b>--Stars!!!<br><br>First and foremost, I have absolutely no idea how to review this book. None. Zero. Zilch. <br><br>I went in to it having absolutely no idea what to expect and I think that's the best way to do it. Just go in blind. Buckle up and enjoy the ride. <br><br>My random thoughts on the book.....<br><br><b>Nora:</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435689ra/880361.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She was fun. She was sexy. She was funny. She was dangerous. She was bold. She was brilliant. <br><br><b>Wesley:</b><br><br>Wesley was<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403144731ra/10046856.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He was so sweet. And pure. I really loved the dynamic between Nora and Wes. They were polar opposites. Best friends. And loved each other in their own special way.<br><br><b>Zach:</b><br><br>Hmm....how do I feel about Zach! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397790332ra/9328483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I actually really liked Zach too. I pretty much waffled the whole book about who I wanted Nora to "end up" with. Not that it mattered because it seems she will forever belong to Soren.<br><br><b>Soren:</b><br><br>Soren who needs to <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/459446.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah, yeah...I get it. He's not going anywhere. But honestly, I'm not a Soren fan. Doesn't help that I don't like the BDSM and D/s elements. Yes, I know....a very prevalent part of the story.<br><br>It might be a deal breaker for me. <br><br>And lastly....<br><br><b>Griffin:</b><br><br>Pretty sure....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385397533ra/7140476.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Only got some small glimpses of you but I'm pretty sure I'm going to love you. <br><br>So who are these people. Well...<br><br>Nora is an erotic author. She she's also <b>THE</b> Dominatrix. She's a Switch. <br><br>Zach is Nora's editor for her new book. <br><br>Wesley is Nora's young, live-in "intern". <br><br>Soren is Soren. <b>The</b> Soren. <br><br>Griffin is another dominant. I have no idea what role he will play in future books, but for whatever reason I just liked him. <br><br>I don't know what to say....other than <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397909836ra/9344914.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was intriguing. It was forbidden. It was sexy. It was different. <br><br>While I admit, I do not care for the BDSM aspects of the storyline, I was still engrossed in both the story and the characters and I can definitely appreciate both. <br><br>I think I will give myself one more book to see if I can handle the BDSM elements before I part ways with Nora and the gang! <br><br>So yeah...there you go. That's all I got. <br><br></span>
