        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2090316304" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6979874473648376377">First read: February 2015 - 5 STARS!<br/>Re-read: October 2019 - <b>5+ STARS!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"The world I live in, you've never seen such freedom."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> Wow, the brilliance of this book when seen from the POV of a re-read was blinding! I appreciated it so much more the second time around.<br/><br/>This went down as a 4-way buddy read with my bestest besties <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/40572117' rel='nofollow noopener'>MONIQUE</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58429822' rel='nofollow noopener'>URSY</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14379473' rel='nofollow noopener'>LEILA</a>. Let me tell you, we had lots to talk about! Thank you, ladies. <3<br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"S&M is as psychological as it is physical and sexual."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <u>
  <b>Wa</b></u></span>
  <span id="freeText6979874473648376377" style="display:none">First read: February 2015 - 5 STARS!<br />Re-read: October 2019 - <b>5+ STARS!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"The world I live in, you've never seen such freedom."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> Wow, the brilliance of this book when seen from the POV of a re-read was blinding! I appreciated it so much more the second time around.<br /><br />This went down as a 4-way buddy read with my bestest besties <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/40572117" rel="nofollow noopener">MONIQUE</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58429822" rel="nofollow noopener">URSY</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14379473" rel="nofollow noopener">LEILA</a>. Let me tell you, we had lots to talk about! Thank you, ladies. &lt;3<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"S&amp;M is as psychological as it is physical and sexual."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <u>
  <b>Warning for <i>The Original Sinners</i> newbies</b>
</u>: <blockquote><b>(1)</b> With no clear Hero, this is not a traditional romance<br /><b>(2)</b> This book is stressful and manipulative <br /><b>(3)</b> This book is so much more enjoyable when you know what's going to happen!</blockquote> Here you have it, my GR friends, the pinnacle of all erotic literature. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Let me show you what life is like lived in the moment. No past, no future, just the one perfect moment you're standing in."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> And I find it fitting that it's not exactly a romance novel. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"He was never my Søren. That's the one thing about being a collared submissive. I was his. He never was mine."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <i>The Siren</i> will make you squirm . . . <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Real sadists don't need to fuck. They need to fuck you up."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> It will make you cringe . . . <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"He's a virgin, Eleanor," he whispered into her ear. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> It has the audacity to mix sex and religion . . .<blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"It's easy to believe in God when you wake up every morning when you wake up every morning knowing you are completely and unconditionally loved."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> And it will make your heart hurt . . .<blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Sometimes love alone doesn't cut it. We can only sacrifice so much of ourselves in a relationship before there's nothing left to love or be loved."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> And Reisz serves it all up via the heroine of all heroines, Nora Sutherlin, who's described by Søren, the King of all sadists, like this: <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You are a creature of appetite. You take what you desire without thought or remorse. And that is how God created you and it is much of why I love you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> It contained everything I love about reading; flawed characters, unreliable narrators, depth, incredible writing, mind-fuckery, taboos, and of course kink.<br /><br />If you haven't read these books yet, I envy you, because Nora and Søren and their world is yours to discover for the first time. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6979874473648376377" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J.m. Darhower" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J.m. Darhower" href="/user/show/1400656-j-m-darhower">J.m. Darhower</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer682808565" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8792159015147430811">I'm not sure if this is common knowledge or not, if I've let this be known, but I am not a big fan of erotica.<br/><br/>Okay, that's not entirely true. I'll rephrase. I'm not a big fan of porn without plot. When the porn becomes the plot, well, then it's just shaky ground and I often see no point in reading it. If I wanted porn, I'd watch porn.<br/><br/>Really, I would. I *like* porn.<br/><br/>So I don't often pick up an erotic book. It's just not my cup of tea usually. I bought The Siren a long time ago in paperback on a re</span>
  <span id="freeText8792159015147430811" style="display:none">I'm not sure if this is common knowledge or not, if I've let this be known, but I am not a big fan of erotica.<br /><br />Okay, that's not entirely true. I'll rephrase. I'm not a big fan of porn without plot. When the porn becomes the plot, well, then it's just shaky ground and I often see no point in reading it. If I wanted porn, I'd watch porn.<br /><br />Really, I would. I *like* porn.<br /><br />So I don't often pick up an erotic book. It's just not my cup of tea usually. I bought The Siren a long time ago in paperback on a rec from a friend (for the life of me, I can't remember who...) and it sat on my shelf for months, staring at me.<br /><br />Last night, on a whim, I picked it up and read the first page.<br /><br />Then the second.<br /><br />Then the third.<br /><br />Then before I knew it, the first chapter was over.<br /><br />And then the second chapter.<br /><br />I had to force myself to go to bed a quarter of the way in.<br /><br />And then today, I picked it back up, unable to stop thinking about it, and got no writing done because I NEEDED TO FINISH THIS DAMN BOOK.<br /><br />In other words, I was Zach. I came into it with a set of judgments, but what I discovered blew me away. This is not porn without plot. This is not porn that becomes the plot. This is a story about flawed but beautiful characters, a fascinating world, that explores different types of relationships and psychological (and even theological) concepts. My mind is still reeling. The Siren is genuinely well-written, artfully laid out, extremely thought out... it's a masterpiece. There's so much depth here. I could never do it justice in a review. I can't even think of a word to describe it. It's beautiful, yet ugly... twisted, yet so clear... it's heartbreaking, yet heartwarming... it's a big ass crazy contradiction.<br /><br />Wow. That's the only word I have for it. Wow.</span>

<div id="review_337449801" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/337449801" />
    <a title="Jane Stewart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3789528-jane-stewart"><img alt="Jane Stewart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346001994p2/3789528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/337449801?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jane Stewart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jane Stewart" href="/user/show/3789528-jane-stewart">Jane Stewart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781459234499" href="/book/show/14623986-the-siren">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3789528-jane-stewart?shelf=erotic-fiction">erotic-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer337449801" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer470271426651899373">2 ½ stars. I want emotional connections. This is more about observing the odd.<br/><br/>STORY BRIEF:<br/>Nora was with Soren for 13 years. He tied her, beat her, and left bruises and blood during sex. She likes rough sex. She still loves him, but she left him 5 years ago. To support her herself, she became a Dominatrix at the local S&M club. She ties and beats clients. She has sex with female clients but not male clients.<br/><br/>Nora published several erotic novels. Now she wants to write a higher quality book and app</span>
  <span id="freeText470271426651899373" style="display:none">2 ½ stars. I want emotional connections. This is more about observing the odd.<br /><br />STORY BRIEF:<br />Nora was with Soren for 13 years. He tied her, beat her, and left bruises and blood during sex. She likes rough sex. She still loves him, but she left him 5 years ago. To support her herself, she became a Dominatrix at the local S&amp;M club. She ties and beats clients. She has sex with female clients but not male clients.<br /><br />Nora published several erotic novels. Now she wants to write a higher quality book and approached a new publisher. Zach is the “high quality editor” who has been assigned to edit and help her. Zach loves his wife Grace, but they are separated.<br /><br />Wesley is a nineteen-year-old college student who lives with Nora. He cooks and runs errands for her in return for room and board. Once in a while Nora visits her ex-lover Soren and comes home with bruises. This upsets Wesley. He loves Nora and asks her not to see Soren.<br /><br />REVIEWER’S OPINION:<br />This is erotic fiction, not romance. We don’t see the development of any relationship that ends happily for Nora. The story begins after she left her lover Soren. It’s about Nora’s relationships with Zach and Wesley. One is a working relationship. The other is a confused loving friendship. Some time is spent with Nora writing her novel. There is one scene that shows Nora working as a Dominatrix.<br /><br />The draw for some readers is Nora being a strong character. And BDSM can be appealing. But for me, I was not turned on by the BDSM because I did not feel the characters having intense emotional desire for the other. There were many sex scenes, but they were mostly bondage and pain, not sex or love. The few scenes between Nora and Soren disappointed me. They were told more than shown. For example (location 1514) “He’d beaten her so hard that night she’d nearly gagged on her own tears. And when he finally gave up on the pain, he’d untied her and let her collapse into his arms. His darkness spent, he laid her in his bed and made love to her so tenderly she’d cried again. In the past when they were still together, he’d talk to her while inside her. Sometimes he would articulate in shocking detail the intensity of his desire for her. Sometimes he would simply claim her, calling her his property, his possession.” (The author does not show the “tenderly” actions. The author does not show the words he used to “articulate in shocking detail the intensity of his desire.”) There were many other sex scenes, not all with Nora. But again, I didn’t feel a character desiring another. Instead I watch humiliation, yes sir submission, and bloody, bruising beatings. Sex scenes include bondage, pain, rear door activity, self pleasuring, two women together, and two men with one woman.<br /><br />I liked Wesley and Zach. My feelings for them were “get away from Nora and you’ll be better off.”<br /><br />I didn’t like Nora. I didn’t feel sympathy. I didn’t care what happened to her. She had no vulnerability (other than “yes sir” when she’s with Soren). I suppose you could say her flaw is being messed up inside, but the why and how of that is not looked at. Zach comes into her life, a normal guy. He’s separated but still in love with his wife. Nora teases and taunts him sexually. She intends to have sex with him, on her terms, in her way, f*** the wife. It’s like “I’m going to expand your horizons by having sex with you.” <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ After Nora has sex with Zach, she is portrayed as being wise and saving Zach’s marriage. Her cure was having him unleash his wildness and bruise her during sex. He is now a changed man who sees his wife differently and returns to her. Personally I didn’t want to give Nora this much credit. Ok, maybe give her a little. I was just glad to see Zach get away from Nora.<br /><br />I’m not sure what was going on with the way Nora treated Wesley. He is a virgin. He hopes to have sex someday, in a meaningful way, with a woman he loves. He loves Nora. She lets him see her naked. She comes to his bed to sleep with him - cuddling, no sex. She lets him undress her and give her a bath. Why does she tempt him in all these ways? He’s young and he works for her. I felt sorry for him. Nora can never be with Wesley because she is physically incapable of vanilla sex (according to her thoughts).<br /><br />This book will shock and push buttons. Nora has sex with fifteen-year-old Michael. She did not know his age at the time. He had problems. Nora does a charitable service and “cures” him by inflicting pain while she has sex with him. He’s now healthier, happier, and grateful. Soren is a Jesuit Priest who had a sexual relationship with Nora for many years while he continued as a priest. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />DATA:<br />Kindle count story length: 8451 (642 KB). Swearing language: strong, including religious swear words. Sexual language: strong. Number of sex and/or bondage pain scenes: about 20. Setting: current day New York City, NY. Copyright: 2012. Genre: erotic fiction.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="470271426651899373" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer2262202235275594601"><b>5 Lesbi-Honest Stars…<i>because lets face it I would totally go there for Nora</i></b><br/><br/>Wow…I am still trying to process this amazing story. <br/><br/>Nora doesn’t just write erotica or perform as a dominatrix - she is a dominatrix. I love her! <br/><br/>She is so many things and contradictions, and I absolutely adore her. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389116749ra/7991245.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Nora has a lot sexy men in her life, and they all want different things from her.   <span id="freeText2262202235275594601" style="display:none"><b>5 Lesbi-Honest Stars…<i>because lets face it I would totally go there for Nora</i></b><br><br>Wow…I am still trying to process this amazing story. <br><br>Nora doesn’t just write erotica or perform as a dominatrix - she is a dominatrix. It is more than job or something she does for fun, it’s who she is. Nora is one of the best heroines I have ever read. I love her! <br><br>She is so many things and contradictions, and I absolutely adore her. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389116749ra/7991245.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nora has a lot sexy men in her life, and they all want different things from her. As the story unfolds we learn so much about her as a character in the way she deals with each of these men. <br><br>As I read this and thought about how I wanted things to go and the best outcome, as I do with all the books I read, I was completely torn. I wasn’t sure how things should go, one minute I thought one way thing and the next chapter, page or paragraph I felt another. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402453310i/9939660.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book had my emotions all jacked up and I swear my heart was beating so fast at the end. I absolutely love when a book messes with me so much that I can’t stop thinking about it when its over. <br><br>I have had this book on my TBR list forever, and I was so scared to read it because I wasn’t sure if I would like it since it isn’t your typical love story. Please don’t be like me….<b>read this</b>, because although it isn’t what we normally call a love story to me it still is one. <br><br>This is the story of love…love for your friends, your past, your passion in life, yourself, for strangers in need, forbidden love…to me its an EPIC story of love. <br><br>I cannot wait to continue on with this series, and believe the hype because this is an amazing story!</span>

<div id="review_1077599358" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1077599358" />

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/17881706-april">April</a>
  </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1077599358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16239334132820961130"><br/><b>“4.25 THE BOMB stars”</b><br/><i>Firstly I want to thank my lovely buddies Eda and Jasmine for being there for me in every stage of this crazy journey!♥♥</i><br/><br/>There are many awesome review’s out there which speaks the beauty of this story! Well, I’m going to use lot of Gif’s and quotes to express my emotions. It might contain spoilers so BEWARE!! Also my apologies in advance, since this is going to be a longer one!<br/><br/>Before I say anything let me take a moment to <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415027675ra/11718060.gif' width='90' height='90' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Yes! I totally deserve it for not picking this holy bo</span>
  <span id="freeText16239334132820961130" style="display:none"><br><b>“4.25 THE BOMB stars”</b><br><i>Firstly I want to thank my lovely buddies Eda and Jasmine for being there for me in every stage of this crazy journey!♥♥</i><br><br>There are many awesome review’s out there which speaks the beauty of this story! Well, I’m going to use lot of Gif’s and quotes to express my emotions. It might contain spoilers so BEWARE!! Also my apologies in advance, since this is going to be a longer one!<br><br>Before I say anything let me take a moment to <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415027675ra/11718060.gif" width="90" height="90" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes! I totally deserve it for not picking this holy book of erotica/S&amp;M sooner!<br><br>Where do I start? There was no end to the awesomeness that is this book and if it was not for the unbelievable characters I wouldn’t have felt emotionally drained after reaching the last page.<br> <br><b>Zachary</b><br><i>Nora: “God, I love a man with big vocabulary.”</i><br>Me: I loved that he was subtle, skeptical, loved the banters between him and Nora. The whole transition of his character was spectacular.<br><br><b>Wesley</b><br><i>Nora: “He made me feel human again…like the kind of person who could stay up too late watching stupid movies and talking.”</i><br>Me: <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419239201ra/13019788.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My baby boy!! His innocence, playfulness and cuteness captured my heart from beginning. He might look stupid to stay with Nora but he’s the only true friend she ever had and loved her for who she was.<br><br><b>Nora</b> <br><i>Zach: “Nora….The siren and the goddess, the ship and the wine-dark sea.”<br>Griffen: “Nora’s not just some smut writer with the wild sex life. She’s the motherfucking queen of the Underground.”<br>Søren: “There are suicide bombers on the Gaza Strip who are less dangerous than you are.”</i><br>Me: <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/626264.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I fucking love this woman. The Siren!! The Bomb!! The Queen Bee♥♥</b> <br>Never met anyone who is sexy, sassy, quirky, dangerous, wild, reckless, generous, feisty and fascinating as her!! I don’t mind going gay for her! Hell, I would let her have her way with me anywhere and everywhere <i>*winks*</i><br><br><b>Søren</b><br>@ 11%<br><br><i>Eda: when you meet Søren...HOMG baby, prepare yourself to fall in love. HARD;)))<br>Me: I’m so excited to meet the legend!!!</i><br><br>@ 30%<br><br><i>Me: WHERE. IS. SØREN??!! I'm 130 pages in so far no sign of him *sobs* please tell me I got the wrong copy *sniffs*<br>Eda: He comes in @50% baby... And he comes in with a BOMB!!!<br>Jasmine: bahahaha. His grand entrance is @ 50% my dear.<br>Me: Let him appear already, I can’t contain my excitement!! </i><br><br>@ 34% <br><br><i>Nora: “Zach, Søren isn’t some boyfriend you have a fight with and then kiss and make up. He’s the invading army you surrender to before it burns your village down.”</i><br><br>@ 40%<br><br><i>Me:</i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417889589ra/12590242.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>@ 49% <br><br><i>Author: All play below had ceased at his presence. He strode down the staircase slowly, imperiously. The world stopped for him. The chaos on the floor fell silent. Everyone everywhere, Nora included, seemed to be holding their breath.<br>Me:</i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419238513ra/13019733.gif" width="140" height="140" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>@50% <br><br><i>Author: If god himself was intimidated by this man, Zach wouldn’t have been surprised.<br>Me: I need a drink. </i><br><br>@95%<br><br><i>Me:</i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384036871ra/6752922.gif" width="360" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>@97%<br><br><i>Me:</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381287815ra/4646212.gif" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know I’m the only one in the history of Siren fan club to say this, but Søren for me is not the epitome of true love! He’s meanest, dominating, egoistic bastard I’ve ever seen! I’ve met my share of sadistic assholes but Søren is the devil himself that guy….he just gives me the creeps! <i>*shudders*</i><br><br>I think I lost some precious friends already *sobs* I tried very hard to <s>love</s> like him but he terrifies the hell out of me!! I promise I’ll read the next book with fresh pair of eyes that is, if he doesn’t Starr in my nightmare: p<br><br><b>Post Siren Trauma</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419238513ra/13019734.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Tiffany Reisz</b><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396340372ra/9119425.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I should hate you for making me not leave my room for the whole day, for skipping my dinner, for staying awake till 3 in the morning, and had me crying myself to sleep BUT I still Love you for writing this masterpiece. Bdsm is not a new genre for me but this was way darker and sinful than any other bdsm story I’ve read!! Very strong plot, complex characters, bitter sweet love, scorching sex and some thought provoking theology.<br><br><b>Rating clarification</b>: for first 50% all I heard was Søren this! Søren that! Everyone from Nora’s past are glorifying their relationship, How they love each other so madly, they are meant to be yadda yadda yadda…...I wanted to live their love rather than being told, there were few flashbacks about their past but all I saw was a sadist part of Søren, Maybe that’s the reason I hate him!! I mean, he gifted <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[a 15 year old virgin boy <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> to her for their anniversary! Can he get any creepier?! In my defense I never got to see the lover side of him. <br><br>On other hand the only love I saw and relished was Wesley’s.<br><blockquote>
<i><b>“It's not morning until you're awake. And it's not night until you're asleep in your bed under my roof. And I could go on and on but hope is a horrible thing, and I love you too much to give you any.”</b></i> </blockquote>Call me a wuss for loving a Kid and not the god, this quote right here is why I love wes!<blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“When Søren touched her she became his. When Wesley touched her, she became herself.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>Søren made Nora what he wants her to be, and Wes loved her despite the siren she is and that for me sealed the deal.<br><br><i>P.S: Thanks for rec’ing this book April♥ </i><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16239334132820961130" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xjhTtVEJnYeX8uSezcPBRHe2alDbHoWMjo9ZIfpKUaHe2UPp3/aNEb/FWnWB7ESZZHMjbxNK96B61WyFqr11Rg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EdkXZDmuJxDUNWyWSXbQzx95I8zDn+1xJq9qoTSlefAJOAc4t1E3hvwC0n0FWVUSDLxq8wvLn13S9V8FZFJdFw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer12860989750891330876">Tiffany Reisz is the <i>USA Today</i>-bestselling author of the Romance Writers of America RITA®-winning Original Sinners series from Harlequin's Mira Books.<br/><br/>Born in Owensboro, Kentucky, Tiffany graduated from Centre College with a B.A. in English. She began her writing career while a student at Wilmore, Kentucky's Asbury Theological Seminary. After leaving seminary to focus on her fiction, she wrote <i>The </i></span>
  <span id="freeText12860989750891330876" style="display:none">Tiffany Reisz is the <i>USA Today</i>-bestselling author of the Romance Writers of America RITA®-winning Original Sinners series from Harlequin's Mira Books.<br /><br />Born in Owensboro, Kentucky, Tiffany graduated from Centre College with a B.A. in English. She began her writing career while a student at Wilmore, Kentucky's Asbury Theological Seminary. After leaving seminary to focus on her fiction, she wrote <i>The Siren</i>, which has sold more than half a million copies worldwide. <br /><br />Tiffany also writes mainstream women's suspense fiction, including <i>The Bourbon Thief</i> (winner of the <i>RT Book Reviews</i> Seal of Excellence Award) and the RITA®-nominated <i>The Night Mark</i>.<br /><br />Her erotic fantasy <i>The Red</i>—self-published under the banner 8th Circle Press—was named an <i>NPR</i> Best Book of the Year and a Goodreads Best Romance of the Month. It also received a coveted starred review from <i>Library Journal</i>. <br /><br />Tiffany lives in Louisville, Kentucky with her husband, author Andrew Shaffer, and two cats. The cats are not writers. </span>
